Williams [LIVE] / Bucureti / 10 decembrie 2011\r\nanother BLAME IT and GINGER GROUP Coop.\r\n\r\nSaul Williams este poet, scriitor i muzician american din Albany, New York. Saul i-a creat un stil muzical unic prin mbinarea dintre poezie i hip-hop alternativ; este liceniat n filosofie i actorie, iar din 1995 devine cunoscut ca un open mic poet, ctignd numeroase premii de slam poetry. Filmul independent Slam, la care Williams a fost i scenograf i actor i-a adus Marele Premiu al Juriului la festivalul de film de la Sundance i Camera Dor la Cannes, premii care l-au consacrat internaional.\r\n\r\nA avut colaborri cu artiti precum Nas, The Fugees, Christian Alvarez, Blackalicious, Erykah Badu, KRS-One, Zack De La Rocha, De La Soul, DJ Krust, dar i poeti precum Allen Ginsberg i Sonia Sanchez. Dup lansarea LP-ului Amethyst Rock Star a avut numeroase show-uri n turneul european al Nine Inch Nails n vara lui 2005, dar i cu The Mars Volta. Trent Reznor a produs urmtorul album Saul Williams, The Inevitable Rise and Liberation of NiggyTardust!.\r\n\r\nCa scriitor, Saul Williams este publicat n The New York Times, Esquire, Bomb Magazine i African Voices. A publicat patru colecii de poezie. Are turnee n universiti i colegii din toata lumea cu show-uri n care mbin muzic i lecturile.\r\n\r\nExplain My Heart, este primul single de pe noul album Volcanic Sunlight, care a fost prezentat pentru prima oara pe 26 ianuarie 2011.\r\n\r\nntrebat care este rolul poeziei n viaa lui, Saul Williams spune: [poezia] este fereastra prin care intr aer, posibiliti de a explora ceea ce simim, ce gndim, cu spaiul de care avem nevoie pentru a vedea mai mult dect ceea ce tim deja. Dac nu m-a deschide posibilitilor necunoscutului a fi pierdut.\r\n\r\nSaul Williams va veni la Bucureti mpreun cu Guillermo Brown [drums], David Stanke [keyboards], Julien Chirol [trombon, percussion, Sands\r\n\r\n7:30pm\r\nSlam\r\nMarc Levin, 1998, 100 min.\r\nFilmmaker Marc Levin won the Grand Jury Prize at the 1998 Sundance Film Festival and the Camera d'Or at Cannes for his feature dramatic directorial debut that helped catalyze the global spoken word movement. Slam, starring Saul Williams, Sonja Sohn (of \"The Wire\") and Bonz Malone, is a prison drama about a young black poet jailed on minor drug charges, who uses his gift with words to regain his freedom. Real-life poets Williams and Sohn wrote their own material. Of the film, Hollywood Reporter wrote, \"Brace yourself for a slam-dunk of a movie, in an in-your-face cinema verite-style that makes Godard's 'Breathless' seem like a cartoon.\" Slam was produced by Levin, New York nightclub owner Henri Kessler, and Prison Life magazine founder Richard Stratton, who spent eight years in prison on marijuana charges. Levin first encountered Williams during a 1996 poetry reading at New York's Nuyorican Poets Cafe.\r\n\r\n9:15pm\r\nQ&A with Saul Williams, Sonja Sohn, Bonz Malone, Bob Holman, Richard Stratton, Liza Jessie Peterson, Marc Levin and moderated by DJ Spooky.\r\n\r\nPART OF:\r\nMasterclass: Marc Levin\r\nThursday, December 5th-Sunday, December 8th\r\n(Identifying and surveying exemplary careers in documentary production through an expansive lens.)\r\nMore info TBA.
